<review>Yet another excellent, independent, local find thanks to Yelp!

This is a kiosk in a quiet Danville strip mall that serves super high-quality coffee. I opted for a hot Turkish coffee to go and it was as intensely bold and rich as I'd expected - and then some. A gentleman who I'm guessing is the husband of the owner was also super explanatory about the coffee and gave me a few sweets to help wash it down.

Look closely and you'll also see Russian and other European sweets and treats for sale along their left side wall. Can't wait to come back and try more of their offerings!</review>< Rate>

< Review>
After searching across the state and internet for shops/delivery services to buy my beans, this place has absolutely met or exceeded all of my expectations.

As someone that prefers the bright acidity and fruitiness of East African coffees I was thrilled to see three Ethiopians (Harrar, Sidamo, and Yirgacheffe) plus a Kenyan AA ranging from $16-21/lb (compared to the $18-24/12oz that many third wave roasters charge for similar offerings) that had all been roasted within the previous week.

The owners were clearly very knowledgeable about their product and were happy to offer tastes and samples based on my preferred brewing method to help inform my future purchases of which I'm sure there will be many.

If you live in the East Bay and care at all about what your coffee tastes like, you owe it to yourself to check out Medleno because of the impeccable quality, value, service, freshness, and variety that they offer.</Review>

<user_name>Dulce</user_name>< date>
1616143537367<//date>
<rating>3</rating>< review>
It pains me to give a review that isn't 5 stars. If you look through my profile you can see that I am generally generous and lenient with my ratings, but I simply cannot in good conscience recommend this salon, and I will explain why.

Simply put, for the price, the quality just is not there. I was a walk-in, so I had to wait, which is to be expected. However, my nail tech left me so that my acrylic could "dry" (and those of you who get your nails done regularly know that acrylic dries very quickly, waiting is not necessary) just so that she could take care of another walk-in who wanted a wax. I get it, they saw money signs, but come on.

Attached are photos of the final outcome of my nails. You read that correctly, the photos are of the *final* outcome, yep, no, not halfway through, FINAL. And if you have any standards at all, you know this isn't good work. I'm sorry, but it just isn't. Honestly, it's a little embarrassing. View them from above and they look... okay, but view them from literally any other angle and they're just not great at all.

Not pictured: really goopy, lumpy topcoat on one nail because it got bumped and the nail tech haphazardly brushed it on, and a white smudge on my thumb nail after the nail tech did the french tip and didn't wait for it to dry before sealing with top coat. They also made my cuticles bleed from cutting them with their tools. I felt rushed, no time was taken at all. Clearly, they care about quantity more than quality.

I do want to take a second to note that my pedicure was a very different story, and I am happy with that result, at the very least. But I will still not return, because I am not in the business of gambling. IMO, coming to this salon is like a game of Russian roulette, maybe you'll get something good? But you might also not. I wouldn't risk it. Go somewhere you know will always take the time and give you your moneys worth.< /review>

<resp>None<//resp><Review>This store used to email out a calendar with their daily deals on it so that you could plan out your visits, but they stopped a few years ago. Now you have to call or drive by to find out what deal they are offering. They also recently stopped offering discounts higher than 50% off specific tags. There were a few times last year when they would mark all clothing for $2 a piece, but then they got a new store manager. Unfortunately, their pricing is too high in my opinion for lower end second hand items ($10 for a Forever21 dress with a tear? No thanks). Plenty of their goods are broken, stained, missing pieces, or just plain unwearable/unusable. If you're going to sell low quality used items, please make sure the price reflects that.< /Review></record></dataset><record>

<name>Amber Krusen</name><Date>1498174363747< /Date><rate>1< /rate>< review>
I have always supported the Salvation Army because I believe they really do help people and do good in the community.  I can't say anything good about this particular location though.  I know one important contribution to the community that they are involved in is allowing people to complete community service in lieu of jailtime there and they also hire a lot of people who are otherwise unemployable because of anger issues or insanity.  Although I support this, it is always disturbing when you have to encounter these slightly crazy "employees".  After cleaning out our garage, we had about a truck bed full of donations but when we got there, they guy said his truck was full for the day and to come back the next day.  We came back the next day with the same truck still full and the guy there started screaming and yelling at us stating that we dumped an old mattress there the night before.  He said he just knew we did it and said that he wouldn't take anything from us because we illegally dumped something there.  We calmly tried to explain that we were not getting rid of a mattress and tried to assure him that our same mattress was on ur bed at home.  He went into a rage and said we couldn't donate anything because he was sure we dumped a mattress there even though there was no proof.  We think he must have stopped taking his meds because his rage and accusations were outlandish and unreasonable for the given situation.  Another guy finally came out and we were able to donate our items, but they wouldn't give us any receipt for the donations because of the raving maniac they had to deal with.  Good luck to the Salvation Army but we will be finding a safer place to donate our items from now on.<//review>
